holoclar is a medicine used to replace damaged cells in the cornea and iris of the eye . limbal cells are the cells that make up the outer layer of your eye , which make up your own cells . this is done by a small surgical procedure , called a biopsy . you will be given a single treatment . the cells will be replaced by autologous limbal cells in your limbus , a type of cell that makes up your eye and the iris . your doctor will tell you the picture of the picture . it is important that you tell your doctor if you have any questions on the use of this medicine , ask your doctor or pharmacist .

micardis belongs to a group of medicines called angiotensin ii receptor antagonists . it works by blocking the activity of the enzyme that causes the blood vessels to narrow . this causes your blood pressure to rise . micardi s blocks the action of the hormone that causes it to relax , which helps your blood vessels relax and reduces the pressure . the high blood pressure can cause damage to blood vessels in several organs , such as heart attack , heart or kidney failure , stroke , blindness , and symptoms of a variety of medications .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . serious side effects tell your doctor immediately if you notice any of the following signs : inflammation , infection , advanced hiv infection or opportunistic infections in the past . infections with a weak immune system can cause symptoms of inflammation . previous infections may have been treated with antiretroviral treatment . these symptoms are caused by the body ' s immune response to fight infections . obvious symptoms are autoimmune disorders , where the immune system attacks the body tissue . this can be a sign of autoimmune disorder , which can lead to autoimmune attacks , causing the body to become inflamed . if these symptoms occur , the body will not respond to descovy . warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse immediately .

victoza contains the active substance liraglutide . it is used to control your blood sugar level . blood sugar is stored in your stomach . if you have heart disease , you should not be given the medicine . your doctor will tell you how much you should be taking . the other ingredients are metformin , another diabetes medicine , and other medicines used to treat diabetes . you should also be given other medicines for diabetes , such as oral antidiabetics such as metformine , pioglitazone , sulfonylurea , sodium - glucose cotransporter 2 inhibitor ( sglt2i ) and insulin .
do not take victoza : - if you are allergic to liraglutide or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor or pharmacist before taking the medicine . warnings : this medicine is not intended for the treatment of a disease of the pancreas . this medicine can be used to treat type 1 diabetes . diabetes is a condition in which the body does not produce enough insulin . diabetic ketoacidosis is an underlying complication of diabetes , high blood sugar . an insulin is made in the body . it is important that you have a good idea to make insulin , but not all of the above apply to you . you should not be on dialysis . tell your doctor immediately if your doctor tells you to stop taking this medicine unless you have severe liver disease
always use this medicine exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are not sure . the recommended dose is 0 . 6 mg , 1 . 2 mg / 1.8 mg . your doctor will check your blood glucose . this is the recommended daily dose . victoza is given under the skin , in a vein , or in muscle . injection is given in thighs , waist , abdomen , and arm . do not inject more than once a day . it is recommended that you do not need to wait for the next injection . you will be given a dose of the medicine . take it as soon as you remember . when you first start to take it , your doctor may decide that you should stop taking it . medical treatment may cause nausea , vomiting and diarrhoea . talk to your doctor
like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . serious side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ) hypoglycaemia : low blood sugar : cold sweat , cool pale skin , headache , fast heartbeat , feeling sick or feeling very hungry , changes in vision or feeling sleepy or weak , nervous , anxious , confused , difficulty concentrating , shaking ( tremor ) - low blood glucose . if you get any of the following side effects talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
keep this medicine out of the sight and reach of children . do not use this medicine after the expiry date which is stated on the pen label and carton after exp . store in a refrigerator ( 2 - 8 ). do not freeze . keep the pen in the original package in order to protect from light . the pen cap should be removed from the refrigerator . this medicine should not be disposed of via wastewater or household waste . ask your pharmacist how to dispose of medicines you no longer use . these measures will help protect the environment .
